***стационарный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рный</a> (13618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statiōnārius</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In the meaning "hospital (relational)", from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стационар.html>стациона́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stacionár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stacionárnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stationary, fixed, permanent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:антенна.html>анте́нна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stacionárnaja</b> antɛ́nna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fixed antenna</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:библиотека.html>библиоте́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stacionárnaja</b> bibliotéka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">permanent library</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hospital
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stacionárnyj</b> bolʹnój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in-patient; hospital patient</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стачк</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strike
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всеобщий.html>всео́бщая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vseóbščaja <b>stáčka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">general strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политический.html>полити́ческая</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческая</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">politíčeskaja (ekonomíčeskaja) <b>stáčka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">political (economic) strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustráivatʹ <b>stáčku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike; go on strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руководить.html>руководи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чкой</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rukovodítʹ <b>stáčkoj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to conduct a strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чек</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svobóda <b>stáček</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">freedom to strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разгонять.html>разгоня́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razgonjátʹ <b>stáčku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disrupt a strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:распространиться.html>распространи́лась</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>); <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:охватить.html>охвати́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stáčka</b> rasprostranílasʹ (na); <b>stáčka</b> oxvatíla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the strike movement has spread (to / over)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стащить.html>стащи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">staščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drag off, to drag down, to pull off, to pull down
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drag into, to pull into
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal, to filch, to pinch, to swipe
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***стая.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стая.html>ста́я</a> (4911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стаꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cattleshed, shelter, tent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стая.html>ста́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stája</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стая.html>ста́и</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стая.html>ста́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стая.html>ста́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flock, herd, pack, troop</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 6a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***ствол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ствол.html>ствол</a> (1580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьvolъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ствол.html>ствол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stvol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ствол.html>ствола́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ствол.html>стволы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ствол.html>стволо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trunk, tree trunk</li>
<li>barrel (of a gun)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gun</li></ol>

***стезя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезя́</a> (21629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стьзꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stĭzja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьdza</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">path</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*stigaˀ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stigʰ-eh₂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stezjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стези́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стези́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> path, way</li></ol>

***стекло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a> (790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьklo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍃𐍄𐌹𐌺𐌻𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stikls</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skljánka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">phial; bottle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steyg-</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stick</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">sklo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stekló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стёкла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стёкол</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glass</li>
<li>chimney (of kerosene lamp)</li>
<li>pane, window, lens</li></ol>

***стеклянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стеклянный.html>стекля́нный</a> (2624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стьклѧнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stĭklęnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьklo, *-ěnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеклянный.html>стекля́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stekljánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>glass, glassy, vitreous</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́вший</a> (22565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***стелить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a> (22565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьlati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stel-</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stl-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>постели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread, to lay, to make <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>сте́лет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma <b>stélet</b> mne postélʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Mum is making a bed for me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линолеум.html>лино́леум</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kogdá búdem <b>stelítʹ</b> linóleum?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">When shall we put linoleum on?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>сте́лет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жесткий.html>жёстко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjáxko stélet, da žóstko spatʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">iron fist in velvet glove, a honey tongue, a heart of gall</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">he makes a soft bed but it's hard to sleep on it</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелиться.html>стели́ться</a> (25540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелиться.html>стели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stelítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread, to spread out, to sprawl</li>
<li>to lie on the ground</li>
<li>to creep <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a plant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to speed over a surface <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of animals and birds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare for bed
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постлели́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postlelítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
